f5254592-1940-4a4f-8722-19c16063e4e9:::||@!@||:::2025-04-14T01:55:24:::||@!@||:::{"id":"f5254592-1940-4a4f-8722-19c16063e4e9","title":{"en":"The Birth of Ramen"},"altTitles":[{"ko":"면면면"},{"ko":"Myeon Myeon Myeon"},{"en":"Era, Noodle, Face"},{"ko-ro":"Myeonmyeonmyeon"},{"ko-ro":"Myunmyunmyun"}],"availableTranslatedLanguages":["en"],"description":{"en":"Early 1960s, South Korea. A time when the nation stood on the edge of hunger and hope, when even one bowl of pig slop stew made from army leftovers could mean survival. In this era of post-war poverty, a man named Jeon Jung-yoon was desperate to give his people a proper, dignified meal. Meanwhile, Kim Hang-pil, a fresh-faced recruit just discharged from KATUSA, joins Jeon’s dream—driven by the thought of someone he loves.
